Vulnerable applications often include web services and other applications that handle user input data without properly controlling it, exposing these systems to significant risks of exploitation by malicious actors.","_key":"4f4b699494850","_type":"span"}],"_type":"block","style":"normal","_key":"0be16d949965"},{"_key":"c9fcb66ff5b8","markDefs":[],"children":[{"_type":"span","marks":[],"text":"Remediation","_key":"abb7b5dbd5e00"}],"_type":"block","style":"h2"},{"markDefs":[],"children":[{"text":"To protect against this vulnerability, we recommend following these measures:","_key":"818e92cfd2d50","_type":"span","marks":[]}],"_type":"block","style":"normal","_key":"2dc6d4bb185b"},{"children":[{"text":"Validate and filter user inputs:","_key":"2081ae5e24200","_type":"span","marks":["strong"]},{"_type":"span","marks":[],"text":" ","_key":"2081ae5e24201"}],"level":1,"_type":"block","style":"normal","_key":"dcda1a20e3e8","listItem":"bullet","markDefs":[]},{"markDefs":[],"children":[{"_type":"span","marks":[],"text":"Rigorously validate and filter the user input before processing it.
